*#########################################################################################################
*#########################################################################################################
* Open-Airspace-file Germany created by Peter Kemme
* please send any comment to peter.kemme[at]gmx.de
*
* effective from 2nd April 2015
* All data and information contained in this data file is provided without guarantee as to their completeness or correctness.   
* Any conclusions drawn from these data and information are the sole responsibility of the user.
* 
* ATTENTION:  Airspace referring to aerodromes outside germany is NOT included in this file !!!
*             e.g. Airspace C LFSB, LSZH, LOWS, etc.
*
*
* The times for the restricted and danger areas (ED-R´s and ED-D´s) are from German-AIP.
* 
*   e.g.    MON-THU     = this area is active from Monday till Thursday 
*           MON-FRI+    = this area is normally active from Monday till Friday. Activation for SAT, SUN and HOL is possible by NOTAM
*                         Special times [e.g. MON 0600 (0500)-FRI 1300(1200)] are NOT indicated!!
*           NOTAM       = this area will only be activated by NOTAM
*           H24         = this area is 24hours every day active including holidays!!
*           HX          = undefined activation times, activation is possible on short notice at every time
*
* Changes to this times can be distributed at every time by NOTAM
*
*
*########################################################################################################
*########################################################################################################
*
*
* changes CW44/13 -> CW10/14
* new coordinates CTR EDFM
* CTR ETNU + ETNJ withdrawn
* CTR ETNT, EDFM, EDLN new dimensions
* airspace F EDWI new dimensions
* new airspace D (not CTR) EDDG, EDLP, EDLW with changed limits of TMZ
* ED-D19 new upper limit
* ED-R10 new upper limit
* ED-R137 divided into sector A and B
* airspace C EDDL new sector overhead EDLN-CTR
* airspace C EDDF new dimension
* 
* changes CW10/14 -> CW18/14
* FIS sectors modifed (southwestern part of germany)
* new "Segelflug-ATIS" Freq around EDDS
* wave window "Thüringer Wald" modified coordinates
*
* changes CW18/14 -> CW50/14
* Implementation of SERA (class F replaced by RMZ)
* new dimensions EDDM-CTR
* new ED-R50
* ED-R18 and 114 withdrawn by NOTAM/NfL
*
* changes CW50/14 -> CW14/15 (AIRAC)
* CTR EDAC downgraded to RMZ, RMZ EDBN new
* CTR EDDK changed coordinates
* D (not CTR) EDFH changed and EDDK new
* TMZ EDFH new
* ED-R76 new coordinates, new sectors, new glidersector "Boxberg"
* ED-R60 new
* C EDDK + EDDF modified
* glider sectors "Loccum" withdrawn
* glider sector "Landshut" new dimension
*
